FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[AvgRating], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[DeletedAt], [p].[Description], [p].[Image], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [p].[ReviewCount], [p].[StockQuantity]
    FROM [products] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND [p].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [p0]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [r].[Id], [r].[Comment], [r].[CreatedAt], [r].[ProductId], [r].[Rating], [r].[UserId], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [a].[AccessFailedCount], [a].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a].[Email], [a].[EmailConfirmed], [a].[LockoutEnabled], [a].[LockoutEnd], [a].[NormalizedEmail], [a].[NormalizedUserName], [a].[PasswordHash], [a].[PersonName], [a].[PhoneNumber], [a].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a].[RefreshToken], [a].[RefreshTokenExpirationDateTime], [a].[SecurityStamp], [a].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a].[UserName], [a].[UserType]

) AS [s] ON [p0].[Id] = [s].[ProductId]
ORDER BY [p0].[Id], [s].[Id]
